    <section class="core-section-container
        core-section-container--with-border border-b-1 border-solid border-color-border-faint py-4 text-color-text" data-test-id="about-us">
<!---->
          <h2 class="core-section-container__title section-title">
            Hakkımızda
          </h2>

<!---->
      <div class="core-section-container__content break-words">
        

          <p class="break-words text-color-text" data-test-id="about-us__description">
              Başarsoft is the leading and pioneering company providing totally tailored solutions in GIS. It was founded in 1997 by a group of passionate group of engineers, professional in GIS in Turkey.

Başarsoft provide GIS solutions in variaty of fields, and focused on Utility Network GIS and Navigation Data Production sector. Main applications in GIS include data management and integration into SCADA, billing, maintenance, SAP, field and Sales Force Management, CRM systems. Başarsoft has been awarded to become regional distributor and solution center for Pitney Bowes, MapInfo Pro GIS solutions, for EMEA region. Başarsoft has developed the largest Infrastructure Network GIS systems for Turkey, including Telecom Wireline &amp; Cable TV Network (basarsoft.com.tr/telcobis), Electricity/Power Grid (basarsoft.com.tr/edabis), Water/Sewage/Stormwater Network (basarsoft.com.tr/sudabis), Natural Gas Network (basarsoft.com.tr/doabis).

Başarsoft is also the leading navigation data and solution provider in Turkey and Northern Cyprus. Başarsoft has been investing in R&amp;D. Special Utility &amp; Navigation Solution for blinds can be given as an example of the projects R&amp;D has developed. Mapbis Inc. is Başarsoft's sister company in USA, opened in 2017. Başarsoft Uganda office registered in Kampala, in 2021.
          </p>

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        attributed-text-segment-list__content-truncated" dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Geçtiğimiz hafta Ankara’da doğal gaz sektör temsilcileriyle Başarsoft Vizyon Buluşmaları’nda bir araya geldik.
 Yerli CBS platformumuz Mapbis Utility, MAKS entegrasyonu, kaçak tarama ve dijital dönüşüm başlıklarında son derece verimli paylaşımlar gerçekleştirdik.
Başarsoft olarak, milli kaynaklarla geliştirdiğimiz teknolojilerle sektörün dijital dönüşümüne öncülük etmekten gurur duyuyoruz.

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Bulut teknolojileri, coğrafi bilgi sistemleriyle buluştu!

Amazon Cloud Day Türkiye’de, <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/company/deloitte?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Deloitte</a> iş birliğiyle AWS Cloud dönüşümünü ve CBS’nin bulut teknolojileriyle entegrasyonunu konuştuk.
Teknoloji Direktörümüz <a class="link" href="https://tr.linkedin.com/in/alper-degirmenci-bb711820?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Alper Degirmenci</a>, “Mapping the Present: How Başarsoft is Shaping the Future with Geospatial Technologies on AWS” sunumuyla geleceğin yenilikçi çözümlerini paylaştı.</p>
